## 3. `_modulate_emotion_switch` -- Full Implementation

**File:** `/home/iamlibai/workspace/claude-project/xiaomei-brain/src/xiaomei_brain/drive/engine.py`, lines 769-827

```python
def _modulate_emotion_switch(self, target: EmotionType, intensity: float) -> tuple:
    """情绪切换惯性：上下文感知的情绪切换。

    三层调制：
    1. 冲突矩阵 — 不同情绪间的切换难度（SADNESS→JOY 很难，FEAR→ANGER 较易）
    2. 个性惯性 — switch_inertia 配置（0.1=好哄，0.9=极其固执）
    3. 激素上下文 — 多巴胺让开心更容易，皮质醇让开心更难、恐惧更容易

    Returns:
        (实际情绪类型, 调整后强度)
    """
    current = self.emotion.type
    if current == EmotionType.NEUTRAL or current == target:
        return (target, intensity)

    # Layer 1: 冲突矩阵
    conflict_pairs = {
        (EmotionType.SADNESS, EmotionType.JOY): 0.8,
        (EmotionType.FEAR, EmotionType.JOY): 0.6,
        (EmotionType.ANGER, EmotionType.JOY): 0.5,
        (EmotionType.JOY, EmotionType.SADNESS): 0.6,
        (EmotionType.JOY, EmotionType.FEAR): 0.5,
        (EmotionType.JOY, EmotionType.ANGER): 0.4,
        (EmotionType.SADNESS, EmotionType.FEAR): 0.2,
        (EmotionType.SADNESS, EmotionType.ANGER): 0.3,
        (EmotionType.FEAR, EmotionType.ANGER): 0.3,
        (EmotionType.ANGER, EmotionType.FEAR): 0.3,
    }
    conflict = conflict_pairs.get((current, target), 0.0)

    # Layer 2: 个性惯性
    conflict *= self.config.emotion.switch_inertia

    # Layer 3: 激素上下文
    if target == EmotionType.JOY:
        if self.hormone.cortisol > 0.5:
            conflict *= 1.3  # 压力大 → 开心更难
        if self.hormone.dopamine > 0.5:
            conflict *= 0.7  # 多巴胺高 → 开心更容易
    elif target == EmotionType.FEAR:
        if self.hormone.cortisol > 0.5:
            conflict *= 0.7  # 皮质醇高 → 恐惧更容易

    # 应用冲突
    adjusted = intensity * (1.0 - max(0.0, min(1.0, conflict)))

    # 阈值判断：候选太弱则维持原情绪（惯性获胜）
    if adjusted < self.emotion.intensity * 0.5:
        return (current, self.emotion.intensity)

    return (target, max(0.0, min(1.0, adjusted)))
```

**Key behavior:** If the destination intensity after inertia reduction is less than 50% of the current emotion's intensity, the switch is rejected and the current emotion persists. The conflict pairs are source-to-target directional -- SADNESS to JOY has the highest conflict (0.8), while SADNESS to FEAR has the lowest (0.2).

## 4. `_modulate_hormone_to_emotion` -- Full Implementation

**File:** `/home/iamlibai/workspace/claude-project/xiaomei-brain/src/xiaomei_brain/drive/engine.py`, lines 729-749

```python
def _modulate_hormone_to_emotion(self, target: EmotionType, intensity: float) -> float:
    """事件时：激素背景调制情绪强度。

    激素是社会性信号的累积——高皮质醇让恐惧更强、让快乐更难。
    返回修正后的 intensity。

    例：设 FEAR 时皮质醇 > 0.6 → 强度放大 20%
        设 JOY 时皮质醇 > 0.6 → 强度缩水 20%，多巴胺 > 0.6 → 强度放大 20%
    """
    if target == EmotionType.FEAR and self.hormone.cortisol > 0.6:
        intensity *= 1.2
    elif target == EmotionType.JOY:
        if self.hormone.cortisol > 0.6:
            intensity *= 0.8
        if self.hormone.dopamine > 0.6:
            intensity *= 1.2
    elif target == EmotionType.ANGER and self.hormone.cortisol > 0.5:
        intensity *= 1.2
    elif target == EmotionType.SADNESS and self.hormone.cortisol > 0.5:
        intensity *= 1.15
    return min(1.0, intensity)
```

**Key behavior:** This modulates the *intensity* of an incoming emotion based on current hormone levels before the emotion is applied. Notably, both `JOY` and `FEAR` use cortisol > 0.6 as threshold (but the elseif means JOY's check comes first -- if JOY and cortisol > 0.6, FEAR's amplification can never execute). The `elif` chain means these are mutually exclusive checks per call.

---

## 5. `_modulate_emotion_to_hormone` -- Full Implementation

**File:** `/home/iamlibai/workspace/claude-project/xiaomei-brain/src/xiaomei_brain/drive/engine.py`, lines 710-727

```python
def _modulate_emotion_to_hormone(self) -> None:
    """每分钟：当前情绪顺向偏置激素。

    情绪持续时，"身体"慢慢跟上——激素随时间被情绪推向同一方向。
    步长很小（0.01 * intensity），一个 intensity=0.7 的情绪
    持续一小时累积约 0.4 的激素偏移，不会压倒事件，但让心情留下痕迹。
    """
    if self.emotion.type == EmotionType.NEUTRAL:
        return
    step = 0.01 * self.emotion.intensity
    if self.emotion.type == EmotionType.FEAR:
        self.hormone.cortisol = min(1.0, self.hormone.cortisol + step)
    elif self.emotion.type == EmotionType.ANGER:
        self.hormone.norepinephrine = min(1.0, self.hormone.norepinephrine + step)
    elif self.emotion.type == EmotionType.JOY:
        self.hormone.dopamine = min(1.0, self.hormone.dopamine + step)
    elif self.emotion.type == EmotionType.SADNESS:
        self.hormone.serotonin = max(0.0, self.hormone.serotonin - step)
```

**Called from:** `tick_minute()` at line 859, only when the emotion is within its duration window (`elapsed <= emotion.duration`) -- i.e., while the emotion is actively being experienced but not yet decaying.

---

## 6. Emotion Decay -- How It Works

The emotion decay pipeline has three phases, all in `tick_minute()` (lines 831-867):

**Phase 1 -- Active emotion (within duration):** When `elapsed <= self.emotion.duration`, the emotion is NOT decaying. Instead, `_modulate_emotion_to_hormone()` is called every minute, pushing hormone levels in the emotion's direction by `0.01 * intensity` (e.g., JOY pushes dopamine up, SADNESS pushes serotonin down). This is the "sustained emotion leaves traces on the body" phase.

**Phase 2 -- Decay:** When `elapsed > self.emotion.duration`, every minute: `self.emotion.intensity *= self.config.emotion.decay_rate` (default `0.95`). So intensity drops 5% per minute -- from 1.0 to 0.1 takes about 45 minutes (`log(0.1)/log(0.95) ~= 45`).

**Phase 3 -- Reset to NEUTRAL:** When `intensity < self.config.emotion.min_intensity` (default `0.1`), the emotion is replaced with `EmotionalState()` (NEUTRAL, intensity=0.0), and logged.

**User activity gate:** If the user has been active within the last 120 seconds (`self._last_user_active`), decay is completely skipped -- emotions don't decay during active conversation.

**Duration values per emotion (from config):**
| Emotion  | Duration |
|----------|----------|
| joy      | 600s (10 min) |
| sadness  | 1800s (30 min) |
| fear     | 300s (5 min) |
| anger    | 600s (10 min) |
| others   | 60s (default) |

**Important asymmetry:** `on_praise()` does NOT accumulate intensity additively when switching from another emotion type -- it checks `if self.emotion.type == EmotionType.JOY` and if not, starts `current_intensity` at 0.0. However `on_goal_failed()` and `on_system_stress()` DO accumulate: `self.emotion.intensity + delta`. This means praise from a SAD state starts fresh joy at the delta value, while consecutive failures compound sadness.

---

## 1. Emotion State Persistence (Save/Load Mechanism)

### DriveStorage (`/home/iamlibai/workspace/claude-project/xiaomei-brain/src/xiaomei_brain/drive/storage.py`)

This is the sole persistence layer for the entire Drive state (including emotion). It writes to and reads from:

- **File path**: `~/.xiaomei-brain/{agent_id}/drive/drive_state.json`

**`save()` method** (line 36): Accepts five state objects (`EmotionalState`, `HormoneState`, `MotivationState`, `DesireState`, `EnergyState`) plus optional `pleasure_data`, `wear_data`, and `token_data`. Each state object's `.to_dict()` is called, and the whole dict is dumped via `json.dump()` to the file.

**`load()` method** (line 70): Reads the JSON file, calls `.from_dict()` on each state object **in-place** (mutating the passed-in objects). The `EmotionalState.from_dict()` on line 52 reconstructs the `EmotionType` enum from the string `"type"` field, plus `intensity`, `created_at`, and `duration`.

**`exists()`** (line 121): Checks if the file exists.

**`clear()`** (line 125): Deletes the file.

### DriveEngine save/load (`/home/iamlibai/workspace/claude-project/xiaomei-brain/src/xiaomei_brain/drive/engine.py`)

- **`save()`** (line 1113): Delegates to `self.storage.save(...)`, passing `self.emotion`, `self.hormone`, `self.motivation`, `self.desire`, `self.energy`, plus serialized pleasure, wear, and token data.

- **`_restore_from_storage()`** (line 125): Calls `self.storage.load(self.emotion, self.hormone, self.motivation, self.desire, self.energy)` at init time. The `load` parameter on `__init__` controls whether restoration happens (default `True`). When `load=False`, state starts with defaults.

- **`load()`** (line 150): Manual re-load, guarded by `_loaded` flag to prevent double-loading.

- **`reset()`** (line 1127): Re-initializes all state to defaults AND calls `self.storage.clear()` to delete the file.

### When save is triggered

The only place `drive.save()` is called is in **`ConsciousLiving.terminate()`** at `/home/iamlibai/workspace/claude-project/xiaomei-brain/src/xiaomei_brain/consciousness/conscious_living.py`, line 1371:
```python
if self.drive:
    self.drive.save()
```
This means emotion (and all Drive state) is only persisted when the agent shuts down cleanly. There is no periodic auto-save during runtime.

**`SelfBody`** -- a proxy class that reads emotion through the `_d()` helper method:
```python
@property
def mood(self) -> str:                 return self._d("emotion.type.value", "平静")
@property
def emotion_intensity(self) -> float:  return self._d("emotion.intensity", 0.0)
```
These are the **read-only proxies through SelfImage**. They are used everywhere SelfImage is used -- L1/L2/L3 consciousness ticks, state summaries, etc.

The core also reads `self.drive.hormone.*` to build a `drive_state_text` string that gets injected into L3 prompts. It does **not** read `emotion.type` or `emotion.intensity` directly as a string -- the emotion flows into the LLM context instead through `si.body.mood` (which proxies `emotion.type.value`).

class EmotionType(Enum):

## 4. Methods That Modify Emotion

### `on_praise(delta=0.3)` -- engine.py line 209
Creates a new `EmotionalState(JOY, ...)`. Modifies emotion directly via reassignment. Also modifies dopamine, oxytocin, serotonin, motivation.

### `on_criticism(delta=0.3)` -- engine.py line 255
Creates a new `EmotionalState(SADNESS, ...)`. Modifies emotion directly. Also modifies cortisol, dopamine, serotonin, norepinephrine, motivation.

### `on_goal_completed(progress=1.0)` -- engine.py line 302
Creates a new `EmotionalState(JOY, ...)` when RPE > 0. Also modifies dopamine, serotonin, cortisol, desire.achievement, desire.survival.

### `on_goal_failed(reason)` -- engine.py line 356
Creates a new `EmotionalState(SADNESS, ...)` with 2x duration. Also modifies cortisol, dopamine, serotonin, desire.achievement, desire.survival.

### `on_goal_progress(progress)` -- engine.py line 400
**Does NOT modify emotion**. Only modifies dopamine via RPE. This is the one that does not touch `self.emotion`.

### `on_curiosity(amount=0.08)` -- engine.py line 491
**Does NOT modify emotion**. Only modifies `self.desire.cognition`.

### `on_insight(amount=0.1)` -- engine.py line 512
**Does NOT modify emotion**. Only modifies `self.desire.expression`.

### `apply_social_signal(signal_type, intensity)` -- engine.py line 533
**Does modify emotion** -- mutates `self.emotion.type`, `.intensity`, `.created_at`, `.duration` in-place (not through `on_praise`/`on_criticism`). The emotion type comes from `SOCIAL_SIGNAL_MAP` (defined in `social_perception.py`), which maps e.g. `user_low_mood` -> `sadness`, `user_angry` -> `anger`.

### `on_system_stress(level, source)` -- engine.py line 956
Creates a new `EmotionalState(FEAR, ...)`. Also modifies cortisol, norepinephrine, energy, desire.survival.

### `on_pleasure_hit()` / `on_pleasure_resisted()` -- engine.py lines 594, 598
**Do NOT modify emotion**. They affect only the PleasureCenter (not EmotionalState).

### Direct mutation in `social_cognition.py` and `inner_voice.py`
Both have `boundary_violation > 0.3` handlers that directly set `self._drive.emotion.type = EmotionType.ANGER` and related fields, bypassing `on_praise`/`on_criticism` entirely.

### `tick_minute()` -- engine.py line 831
**Decays emotion**, not creates. Multiplies `self.emotion.intensity *= decay_rate`. If below `min_intensity`, resets `self.emotion = EmotionalState()` (NEUTRAL).

### `_modulate_emotion_to_hormone()` -- engine.py line 710
Reads `self.emotion.type` and `self.emotion.intensity`. Does NOT modify emotion; it pushes emotion's effects into hormone values.

### Summary table of whether each method touches `self.emotion`:

| Method | Modifies emotion? | How? |
|--------|-------------------|------|
| `on_praise` | YES | New EmotionalState(JOY, ...) |
| `on_criticism` | YES | New EmotionalState(SADNESS, ...) |
| `on_goal_completed` | YES | New EmotionalState(JOY or SADNESS, ...) |
| `on_goal_failed` | YES | New EmotionalState(SADNESS, ...) |
| `on_goal_progress` | NO | Only hormone changes |
| `on_curiosity` | NO | Only desire.cognition |
| `on_insight` | NO | Only desire.expression |
| `apply_social_signal` | YES | In-place mutation of emotion.type/intensity/created_at/duration |
| `on_system_stress` | YES | New EmotionalState(FEAR, ...) |
| `on_pleasure_hit` | NO | PleasureCenter only |
| `on_pleasure_resisted` | NO | PleasureCenter only |
| `tick_minute` | YES | Decays intensity, may reset to NEUTRAL |
| `reset` | YES | New EmotionalState() |
| `_restore_from_storage` | YES | `storage.load()` calls `emotion.from_dict()` |

## Summary: The Complete Emotion Data Flow

```
                              [PERSISTENCE LAYER]
                                    |
  drive_state.json  <-- DriveStorage.save/load -->  EmotionalState.to_dict()/from_dict()
                                    |
                                    v
                            [DriveEngine]
                           holds: self.emotion (EmotionalState)
                                    |
         +--------------------------+-----------------------------+
         |                          |                             |
   [EVENT WRITERS]           [TICK DECAY]              [READERS / PROXIES]
         |                          |                             |
  on_praise()               tick_minute()              SelfBody.mood (proxy)
  on_criticism()             decays intensity          SelfBody.emotion_intensity
  on_goal_completed()        may reset -> NEUTRAL           |
  on_goal_failed()                                     consciousness/core.py
  apply_social_signal()                                (L3 deep burn prompt,
  on_system_stress()                                     _detect_emotion_spike)
         |                                                    |
  InnerVoice._apply_drive_events()                    living_commands.py
  SocialCognition._apply_drive_events()               (CLI `/drive` display)
  (both: boundary_violation -> direct mutation)
         |
  EmotionProcessor (dream/emotion_processor.py)
  (modifies desire/hormone only, NOT emotion type)
```

Key architectural observations:

1. **Single persistence point**: Emotion state is only saved to disk via `DriveStorage.save()` which is only called in `ConsciousLiving.terminate()`. There is no periodic auto-save during runtime.

2. **Two mutation patterns**: The engine methods (`on_praise`, `on_criticism`, etc.) create entirely new `EmotionalState` objects. But `apply_social_signal()` and the `boundary_violation` handlers in `InnerVoice`/`SocialCognition` mutate `self.emotion` **in-place** (setting `.type`, `.intensity`, `.created_at`, `.duration` individually).

3. **Read path to LLM**: Emotion does not flow into the regular conversation LLM context via context_assembler. It flows into the L3 deep-burn consciousness prompt via `si.body.mood` (which resolves to `drive.emotion.type.value`) and `si.body.emotion_intensity`.

4. **No tests exist** for any part of the drive/emotion system.</result>

**[19:47:09] 🤖助手**

找到 bug 了。`SelfBody._d()` 方法是按 DriveEngine 的属性链遍历的。

```python
# mood 属性走的是："emotion.type.value"
# → getattr(drive, "emotion") → EmotionalState
# → getattr(EmotionalState, "type") → EmotionType
# → .value → "joy"

# 但我写的 emotions_dict 是："emotions"
# → getattr(drive, "emotions") → 没有这个属性！
```

路径错了，应该是 `"emotion.emotions"`。修复：

**[19:48:29] 🟥用户**

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user is building a mixed/compound emotion system for the xiaomei-brain agent. The original mono-emotion model had a single `type` + `intensity` slot that caused SIGNAL (social signals like `user_angry` → FEAR) and EVENTS (drive events like `boundary_violation` → ANGER) to overwrite each other. The user wanted mixed emotions where both coexist (e.g., anger=0.81 + fear=0.64 simultaneously), with dominant emotion determination and compound rendering in the system prompt.

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - **Mixed/Compound Emotion Model**: `EmotionalState.emotions: dict[str, float]` replacing scalar `type` + `intensity`
   - **Backward-compat properties**: `type` and `intensity` as computed properties returning dominant emotion
   - **`SelfBody._d(path, default)` method**: Traverses DriveEngine attribute chain. Path `"emotion.emotions"` means `getattr(drive, "emotion")` → EmotionalState, then `getattr(emotion, "emotions")` → dict
   - **`add_emotion(name, intensity)`**: Merges by max per key (doesn't overwrite other emotions)
   - **`decay_all(rate)`**: All emotions decay together, removed below 0.08 threshold
   - **`_modulate_emotion_switch()`**: Now uses `dominant()` instead of `self.emotion.type`, blocking threshold removed
   - **`_describe_mixed_emotions(emotions: dict)`**: Renders compound labels like "非常愤怒，紧张焦虑"
   - **Old format migration**: `from_dict()` detects `{"type": "joy", "intensity": 0.5}` vs `{"emotions": {...}}` format
   - **Three render files** (v1/v2/v3) each got identical `_describe_mixed_emotions()` function
   - **SIGNAL → EVENTS execution order** was swapped in previous session (SIGNAL first, EVENTS second to overwrite), now moot with mixed emotions

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/drive/state.py`** — Core data model change. Replaced `@dataclass EmotionalState` with plain class using `emotions: dict[str, float]` storage plus backward-compat `type`/`intensity` properties.
     ```python
     class EmotionalState:
         def __init__(self, emotions=None, type=None, intensity=0.0, created_at=0.0, duration=60.0):
             if emotions:
                 self.emotions = dict(emotions)
             elif type is not None and type != EmotionType.NEUTRAL:
                 key = type.value if isinstance(type, EmotionType) else type
                 self.emotions = {key: intensity}
             else:
                 self.emotions = {}
             self.created_at = created_at
             self.duration = duration

         @property
         def type(self) -> EmotionType:
             if not self.emotions: return EmotionType.NEUTRAL
             return EmotionType(max(self.emotions, key=self.emotions.get))

         @property
         def intensity(self) -> float:
             if not self.emotions: return 0.0
             return max(self.emotions.values())

         def add_emotion(self, name, intensity):
             clamped = max(0.0, min(1.0, intensity))
             if clamped < 0.05: return
             existing = self.emotions.get(name, 0.0)
             self.emotions[name] = max(existing, clamped)
             self.created_at = time.time()

         def decay_all(self, rate):
             for key in list(self.emotions):
                 self.emotions[key] *= rate
                 if self.emotions[key] < 0.08: del self.emotions[key]

         def is_empty(self): return not self.emotions

         def dominant(self):
             if not self.emotions: return ("neutral", 0.0)
             name = max(self.emotions, key=self.emotions.get)
             return (name, self.emotions[name])

         def to_dict(self):
             return {"emotions": dict(self.emotions), "created_at": self.created_at, "duration": self.duration}

         def from_dict(self, data):
             if "emotions" in data:
                 self.emotions = data["emotions"]
             else:
                 # Old format migration
                 old_type = data.get("type", "neutral")
                 old_intensity = data.get("intensity", 0.0)
                 self.emotions = {old_type: old_intensity} if old_type != "neutral" and old_intensity > 0 else {}
             self.created_at = data.get("created_at", 0.0)
             self.duration = data.get("duration", 60.0)
     ```

   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/drive/engine.py`** — All writers + modulation + decay updated. Changed 6 `on_*` methods from `EmotionalState(type=..., intensity=...)` to `add_emotion()`. Changed `apply_social_signal` from in-place mutation to `add_emotion()`. Changed `_modulate_emotion_to_hormone` to iterate all emotions. Changed `_modulate_emotion_switch` to use `dominant()` and removed blocking threshold. Changed `tick_minute` to use `decay_all()`.
     Key pattern across all writers:
     ```python
     # Before:
     self.emotion = EmotionalState(type=actual_type, intensity=intensity, created_at=time.time(), duration=...)
     # After:
     if intensity >= 0.05:
         self.emotion.add_emotion(actual_type.value, intensity)
         self.emotion.duration = ...
     ```

   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/metacognition/inner_voice.py`** — Boundary violation handler changed from direct mutation to `add_emotion()`.
     ```python
     # Before:
     self._drive.emotion.type = EmotionType.ANGER
     self._drive.emotion.intensity = min(1.0, boundary * 0.9)
     # After:
     anger_intensity = min(1.0, boundary * 0.9)
     self._drive.emotion.add_emotion("anger", anger_intensity)
     ```

   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/metacognition/social_cognition.py`** — Same boundary handler fix as inner_voice.py.

   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/consciousness/self_modules.py`** — Added `emotions_dict` property to `SelfBody`. **BUG FOUND**: Initial path was wrong.
     ```python
     # WRONG (initial commit):
     def emotions_dict(self) -> dict: return self._d("emotions", {})
     # CORRECT (final fix, uncommitted):
     def emotions_dict(self) -> dict: return self._d("emotion.emotions", {})
     ```
     Reason: `_d(path, default)` traverses DriveEngine attributes with `getattr(val, attr)` per path segment. `"emotion.emotions"` correctly gets DriveEngine.emotion (EmotionalState) → EmotionalState.emotions (dict). `"emotions"` would try `getattr(DriveEngine, "emotions")` which doesn't exist.

   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/consciousness/workspace/render_consciousness_v3.py`** — Added `_describe_mixed_emotions()` and updated `_render_body()`.
     ```python
     def _describe_mixed_emotions(emotions: dict) -> str:
         if not emotions: return "平静"
         label_map = {
             "joy": {0.7: "非常开心", 0.4: "开心", 0.1: "有些愉悦"},
             "sadness": {0.7: "非常悲伤", 0.4: "低落", 0.1: "有些消沉"},
             "fear": {0.7: "非常恐惧不安", 0.4: "紧张焦虑", 0.1: "有些不安"},
             "anger": {0.7: "非常愤怒", 0.4: "生气", 0.1: "有些烦躁"},
             "surprise": {0.7: "非常震惊", 0.4: "有些惊讶", 0.1: "微微一愣"},
             "disgust": {0.7: "非常反感", 0.4: "感到排斥", 0.1: "有些不适"},
         }
         parts = []
         for name, intensity in sorted(emotions.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True):
             thresholds = label_map.get(name, {0.7: name, 0.1: name})
             label = name
             for threshold, lbl in sorted(thresholds.items(), reverse=True):
                 if intensity >= threshold: label = lbl; break
             parts.append(label)
         return "，".join(parts) if len(parts) > 1 else parts[0]
     ```
     `_render_body()` changed from `_describe_emotion(_mood, _emotion_intensity)` to `_describe_mixed_emotions(_emotions)` using `bo.emotions_dict`.

   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/consciousness/workspace/render_consciousness_v1.py`** — Same `_describe_mixed_emotions()` + `_render_body()` update.

   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/consciousness/workspace/render_consciousness_v2.py`** — Same function added, updated both `_v1_body()` and `_render_body()` LOW detail path.

   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/consciousness/living_commands.py`** — CLI `/drive` now shows all active emotions:
     ```python
     e = living.drive.emotion
     if e.is_empty(): print("  平静")
     else:
         for name, intensity in sorted(e.emotions.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True):
             print(f"  {name}: {intensity:.2f}")
     ```

   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/consciousness/conscious_living.py`** — Log output updated to show all emotions (same pattern as living_commands.py).

**[19:48:49] 🤖助手**

已提交 `d0bcd21`。这是 `self_modules.py` 第 249 行的一个单字符修复：`_d("emotions", {})` → `_d("emotion.emotions", {})`。

原因：`_d(path)` 按 `.` 分段遍历 `DriveEngine` 的属性链。`"emotion.emotions"` 正确解析为 `drive.emotion`（→ EmotionalState）→ `.emotions`（→ dict）。原来的 `"emotions"` 尝试直接 `getattr(DriveEngine, "emotions")`，但字段名是单数的 `emotion`，所以永远返回空 dict `{}`。

重新启动 agent 测试一下，发送一条冒犯消息，system prompt 中的心情应该显示为"非常愤怒，紧张焦虑"而非"平静"。
